\newlength{\parindentOriginal}
\setlength{\parindentOriginal}{\parindent}
\setlength{\parindent}{0mm}
\begin{tikzpicture}
    \begin{scope}[x={(0mm,\textwidth)},y={(0,45mm)}]
		\begin{axis}[%
				title={$V_{in} = \SI{0.5}{\volt}${,} $f_{s} = \SI{32}{\kilo\hertz}$},
				height=45mm,
				width=\textwidth,
				grid=both,
				xlabel=Time (\si{\second}),
				ylabel=Voltage (\si{\volt}),
				%change x base = true,
				%x SI prefix = micro,
			]
			% For digital measurements
			%\addplot[-,blue] table[x=Time, y=Ampl,col sep=comma] {data/both/chip08/chip08-256kHz-1.5V.dat};
			\addplot[only marks,mark size=1pt,plotColor1] 
				table[x=Time, y=Ampl,col sep=comma] {data/both/chip01/chip01-032kHz-0.5V.dat};
			\addplot[only marks,mark size=1pt,plotColor2]

			\addplot[only marks,mark size=1pt,plotColor6]
